           How Do Spam Callers Spoof Phone Numbers to Appear Local?
          </a>
         </h3>
         <p class="bc-excerpt">
          Spotting spam calls is tricky, especially if it looks like a call from a local number.
         </p>

  <script>
   document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
            var queryString = window.location.search || '';
            var keyValPairs = [];
            var params      = {};

            queryString     = queryString.substr(1);
            if (queryString.length)
            {
                keyValPairs = queryString.split('&');
                for (var i = 0; i < keyValPairs.length; i++)
                {
                    var key = keyValPairs[i].split('=')[0];
                    if (!key.length) continue;
                    if (typeof params[key] === 'undefined')
                        params[key] = [];
                    params[key].push(keyValPairs[i].split('=')[1]);
                }

                if (params['view'] !== undefined) {
                    if (params['view'] == "list" || params['view'] == "lista") {
                        valnet_cookie.set("view",params['view']);
                    }
                }

                var campaign = null;
                if (params['utm_source'] !== undefined) {
                    campaign = params['utm_source'];
                }
                if (campaign !== null) {
                    valnet_cookie.set("campaign",campaign);
                }
            }
        });
  </script>

   console.log('viewType: direct');

        console.log('device: desktop');
  </script>
 </body>
</html>
